# Complete Action Ledger

<span class="cg-badge cg-atlas">Atlas and indexes</span>

## Lead

The Complete Action Ledger lists every extracted operation, action, reaction, result, plan, and
major sub-event heading from the PDF-derived event sections.

- [[1981 Action Ledger]] - 373 action nodes

- [[1986 Action Ledger]] - 228 action nodes
- [[1987 Action Ledger]] - 508 action nodes
- [[1988 Action Ledger]] - 340 action nodes
- [[1989 Action Ledger]] - 438 action nodes
